I am hoping that even with Jews in his family, Trump will begin to recognize that Jewish interests do not coincide with the interests of most Europeans or Euro-Americans. This is because Jews invariably promote policies that are \u201cgood for Jews\u201d and bad for everyone else. This has always been the problem.\n\nI hope Trump will come to realize, for example, that his cheerleading for Israel contradicts his policy of \u201cAmerica First\u201d.\n\nDecades ago I saw a book by a German Jewish woman in a bookstore. In those days, before I became desensitized to the anti-German hatred, these things had a greater impact on me. This woman in the book, the female narrator, had married a German who was in the National Socialist party. She\u2019d had children by him. From browsing through the book, I gathered that her German husband stayed loyal to her throughout their marriage, even though his wife was Jewish and their children regarded as Jews. The German husband, like most other National Socialists at that time, was of course keenly aware of the so-called \u201cJewish Question\u201d. And so having a Jewish wife and children must have been a tricky business for him.\n\nIn any case, the Jewess writing the book, instead of reciprocating her German husband\u2019s love and loyalty toward her, chose to betray him in print by denouncing him to the world as a \u201cNazi\u201d. This was what the book was all about: righteous Jewish lady turns and tears her nasty German husband apart for being a \u201cNazi\u201d \u2014 after having being supported by him for several years, treated with exemplary kindness by him, and given children by him.\n\nInstead of gratitude, spouse betrayal. One has to feel sorry for that man. He was probably aware of the profound effect his Jewish wife was having on his children.\n\nIf I mention this case here, it\u2019s because we have a parallel situation in Donald Trump. Trump may come to recognize in time the profound effect on his daughter Ivanka of having married a Jew, Jared Kushner, and the psychological effects of being surrounded by Jewish grandchildren.\n\nWill Trump, too, be betrayed by the Jews around him? Will be forced to do what he doesn\u2019t want to do, under Jewish pressure?\n\n\u2014 \u00a7 \u2014\n\nAs for George Soros, the archetypal Jew, it has been said: \u201cHe is trying to create a race war because, all of a sudden in the last 90 days, it\u2019s become possible for the 99 per cent to unite around Donald Trump against the 1 per cent.\u201d\n\nI\u2019m glad a minority noticed that, but it isn\u2019t just Soros and it has been going on for years. 300lb thug Michael Brown in Ferguson, Trayvon Martin in Florida, and other black criminals have been elevated to sainthood, while whites are portrayed as the evil overlords. Thus, Black Lives Matter makes anti-white racist statements; meanwhile, blacks continue their attacks on whites (and Asians) on the streets.\n\nAnd who is egging the blacks on? Answer: George Soros and his Jews.\n\nWhat the tens of millions of anti-whites don\u2019t know, amid all the anti-white Jewish propaganda in the media, is that it was American whites who let them into this country in the first place. Whites didn\u2019t have to do that, but they did \u2014 under intense Jewish pressure that had been going on for several decades. This was when America passed the fateful Hart-Cellar act in 1965. After 1965, as a result, non-Whites began to pour into America in ever increasing numbers, with American Jews acting as cheerleaders for multiculturalism.\n\nLetting these minorities into the country so recklessly and foolishly, in such ridiculously large numbers, was not a good idea. It was the dumbest thing America ever did. Why? Because these very same minorities have now become a major problem. They have turned against their White hosts who gave them the hospitality of a new life in a new country. These minorities now attack whites as \u201cracists\u201d and increasingly rape White women in \u201crace revenge\u201d.\n\nThey have bitten the hand that fed them.\n\nIt\u2019s also worth noting that Soros emigrated from Hungary to the US at the exact time his fellow Hungarian Jews were killing and torturing Hungarians, until the Hungarians rose up against the Jews. Could it happen here? Certainly it could happen, though perhaps not yet.\n\nWorld Jewry wields enormous power, not just in the US, but in most western countries. Right now, Hungary is the only European nation taking stringent measures to limit the number of illegal immigrants pouring into Europe. They have even gone one step further: they are now granting asylum status to other White Europeans, such as Germans and Swedes, who are fleeing from the multicultural hordes who are taking over their countries and making life increasingly impossible for them.\n\nWatch this 6-minute David Irving clip please. It is not without relevance to the subject we have been discussing. It shows what can happen to a country that lets in large numbers of Jews: complete takeover by Jews.\n\nHungary, 1956 . . . class=\"main-content-inner col-sm-12 col-md-8\">\n\n\t<div id=\"primary\" class=\"content-area\">\n\t\t<main id=\"main\" class=\"site-main\" role=\"main\">\n\n\t\t\n<article id=\"post-61343\" class=\"post-61343 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-other-writers tag-george-soros\">\n\t\t<div class=\"post-inner-content\">\n\t\t<header class=\"entry-header page-header\">\n\n\t\t\t<h1 class=\"entry-title \">Who Is Destroying America?</h1>\n\n\t\t\t<div class=\"entry-meta\">\n\t\t\t\t<span class=\"byline\"> <i class=\"fa fa-user fa-2x\"></i> <span class=\"author vcard\"><a class=\"url fn n\" href=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/author/admin/\">Admin</a></span></span><span class=\"posted-on\"><i class=\"fa fa-calendar\"></i> <a href=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/2017/who-is-destroying-america/\" rel=\"bookmark\"><time class=\"entry-date published\" datetime=\"2017-02-28T12:28:45+00:00\">February 28, 2017</time></a></span>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"cat-links\"><i class=\"fa fa-folder-open-o\"></i>\n\t\t\t\t\t <a href=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/category/other-writers/\" rel=\"category tag\">Other Writers</a>\t\t\t\t</span>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t</div><!-- .entry-meta -->\n\t\t</header><!-- .entry-header -->\n\n\t\t<div class=\"entry-content\">\n\t\t\t<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><strong>By Petrus Germanicus</strong><br/>\n<strong>(aka &#8216;Peter&#8217;)</strong></p>\n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-61345\" src=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/Ca2_sigUsAApVKE.jpg.pagespeed.ce.cCjCdeaV10.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"600\" height=\"483\" srcset=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/Ca2_sigUsAApVKE.jpg 600w, https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/Ca2_sigUsAApVKE-150x121.jpg 150w, https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/Ca2_sigUsAApVKE-300x242.jpg 300w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 600px) 100vw, 600px\"/></p>\n<h2 style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"color: #800000;\">DESTROYING \u00a0AMERICA</span></h2>\n<p><strong>Trump&#8217;s anti-Iran bashing and pro-Israel rhetoric is a genuine cause for concern. I am hoping that even with Jews in his family, Trump will begin to recognize that Jewish interests do not coincide with the interests of most Europeans or Euro-Americans. This is because Jews invariably promote policies that are &#8220;good for Jews&#8221; and bad for everyone else. This has always been the problem.</strong><span id=\"more-61343\"></span></p>\n<p>I hope Trump will come to realize, for example, that his cheerleading for Israel contradicts his policy of \u201cAmerica First\u201d.</p>\n<p>Decades ago I saw a book by a German Jewish woman in a bookstore. In those days, before I became desensitized to the anti-German hatred, these things had a greater impact on me. This woman in the book, the female narrator, had married a German who was in the National Socialist party. She&#8217;d \u00a0had children by him. From browsing through the book, I gathered that her German husband stayed \u00a0loyal to her throughout their marriage, even though his wife was Jewish and their children regarded as Jews. The German husband, like most other National Socialists at that time, was of course keenly aware of the so-called &#8220;Jewish Question&#8221;. And so having a Jewish wife and children must have been a tricky business for him.</p>\n<p>In any case, the Jewess writing the book, instead of reciprocating her German husband&#8217;s love and loyalty toward her, chose to betray him in print by denouncing him to the world as a &#8220;Nazi&#8221;. This was what the book was all about: righteous Jewish lady turns and tears her nasty German husband apart for being a &#8220;Nazi&#8221; \u2014 after having being supported by him for several years, treated with exemplary kindness by him, and given children by him.</p>\n<p>Instead of gratitude, spouse betrayal. One has to feel sorry for that man. He was probably aware of the profound effect his Jewish wife was having on his children.</p>\n<p>If I mention this case here, it&#8217;s because we have a parallel situation in Donald Trump. Trump may come to recognize in time the profound effect on his daughter Ivanka of having married a Jew, Jared Kushner, and the psychological effects of being surrounded by Jewish grandchildren.</p>\n<p>Will Trump, too, be betrayed by the Jews around him? Will be forced to do what he doesn&#8217;t want to do, under Jewish pressure?</p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\">\u2014 \u00a0\u00a7 \u00a0\u2014</p>\n<p>As for George Soros, the archetypal Jew, it has been said: \u201cHe is trying to create a race war because, all of a sudden in the last 90 days, it\u2019s become possible for the 99 per cent to unite around Donald Trump against the 1 per cent.\u201d</p>\n<p>I\u2019m glad a minority noticed that, but it isn\u2019t just Soros and it has been going on for years. 300lb thug Michael Brown in Ferguson, Trayvon Martin in Florida, and other black criminals have been elevated to sainthood, while whites are portrayed as the evil overlords. Thus, Black Lives Matter makes anti-white racist statements; meanwhile, blacks continue their attacks on whites (and Asians) on the streets.</p>\n<p>And who is egging the blacks on? Answer: George Soros and his Jews.</p>\n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-61344\" src=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/648x441xgeorge-soros-quote-1024x697.jpg.pagespeed.ic.1olTTZMYhZ.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"648\" height=\"441\" srcset=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/george-soros-quote-1024x697.jpg 1024w, https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/george-soros-quote-150x102.jpg 150w, https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/george-soros-quote-300x204.jpg 300w, https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/george-soros-quote-768x523.jpg 768w, https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/george-soros-quote-600x408.jpg 600w, https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/george-soros-quote.jpg 1080w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 648px) 100vw, 648px\"/></p>\n<p>What the tens of millions of anti-whites don\u2019t know, amid all the anti-white Jewish propaganda in the media, is that it was American whites who let them into this country in the first place. Whites didn&#8217;t have to do that, but they did \u2014 under intense Jewish pressure that had been going on for several decades. This was when America passed the fateful Hart-Cellar act in 1965. After 1965, as a result, non-Whites began to pour into America in ever increasing numbers, with American Jews acting as cheerleaders for multiculturalism.</p>\n<p>Letting these minorities into the country so recklessly and foolishly, in such ridiculously large numbers, was not a good idea. It was the dumbest thing America ever did. Why? Because these very same minorities have now become a major problem. They have turned against their White hosts who gave them the hospitality of a new life in a new country. These minorities now attack whites as \u201cracists\u201d and increasingly rape White women in &#8220;race revenge&#8221;.</p>\n<p>They have bitten the hand that fed them.</p>\n<p>It\u2019s also worth noting that Soros emigrated from Hungary to the US at the exact time his fellow Hungarian Jews were killing and torturing Hungarians, until the Hungarians rose up against the Jews. Could it happen here? Certainly it could happen, though perhaps not yet.</p>\n<p>World Jewry wields enormous power, not just in the US, but in most western countries. Right now, Hungary is the only European nation taking stringent measures to limit the number of illegal immigrants pouring into Europe. They have even gone one step further: they are now granting asylum status to <em>other</em> White Europeans, such as Germans and Swedes, who are fleeing from the multicultural hordes who are taking over their countries and making life increasingly impossible for them.</p>\n<p>Watch this 6-minute David Irving clip please. It is not without relevance to the subject we have been discussing. It shows what can happen to a country that lets in large numbers of Jews: <em>complete takeover by Jews.</em></p>\n<p>Hungary, 1956 . . . America, 2056?</p>\n<h4 style=\"text-align: center;\"><strong><span style=\"color: #800000;\">VIDEO : 5.55 mins</span></strong></h4>\n<p><iframe width=\"648\" height=\"486\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/GvcfRXqkYuk?start=108&#038;feature=oembed\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen></iframe></p>\n<!-- Simple Share Buttons Adder (6.3.4) simplesharebuttons.com --><div class=\"ssba ssba-wrap\"><div style=\"text-align:center\">Like this? Burns</p>\n<p>More and more, we are seeing citizens being invited to \u201cparticipate\u201d in various forms of meetings, councils, or boards to \u201chelp determine\u201d public policy in one field or another. They are supposedly being included to get \u201dinput\u201d from the public to help officials make final decisions on taxes, education, community growth or whatever the particular subject matter might be.</p>\n<p>Sounds great, doesn\u2019t it? Unfortunately, surface appearances are often deceiving.</p>\n<p>You, Mr. or Mrs. Citizen, decide to take part in one of these meetings.</p>\n<p>Generally, you will find that there is already someone designated to lead or \u201cfacilitate\u201d the meeting. Supposedly, the job of the facilitator is to be a neutral, non-directing helper to see that the meeting flows smoothly.</p>\n<p>Actually, he or she is there for exactly the opposite reason: to see that the conclusions reached during the meeting are in accord with a plan already decided upon by those who called the meeting.</p>\n<p><strong>The process used to \u201cfacilitate\u201d the meeting is called the Delphi Technique.</strong> </p>\n<p>This Delphi Technique was developed by the RAND Corporation for the U.S. Department of Defense back in the 1950s. It was originally intended for use as a psychological weapon during the cold war.<br/>\nHowever, it was soon recognized that the steps of Delphi could be very valuable in manipulating ANY meeting toward a predetermined end.</p>\n<p>How does the process take place? The techniques are well developed and well defined.</p>\n<p>First, the person who will be leading the meeting, the facilitator or Change Agent must be a likable person with whom those participating in the meeting can agree or sympathize.</p>\n<p>It is, therefore, the job of the facilitator to find a way to cause a split in the audience, to establish one or a few of the people as \u201cbad guys\u201d while the facilitator is perceived as the \u201cgood guy.\u201d</p>\n<p>Facilitators are trained to recognize potential opponents and how to make such people appear aggressive, foolish, extremist, etc. Once this is done, the facilitator establishes himself or herself as the \u201cfriend\u201d of the rest of the audience.</p>\n<p>The stage is now set for the rest of the agenda to take place.</p>\n<p>At this point, the audience is generally broken up into \u201cdiscussion\u2014or \u2018breakout\u2019\u2014groups\u201d of seven or eight people each. Each of these groups is to be led by a subordinate facilitator.</p>\n<p>Within each group, discussion takes place of issues, already decided upon by the leadership of the meeting. Here, too, the facilitator manipulates the discussion in the desired direction, isolating and demeaning opposing viewpoints.</p>\n<p>Generally, participants are asked to write down their ideas and disagreements with the papers to be turned in and \u201ccompiled\u201d for general discussion after the general meeting is reconvened.</p>\n<p><strong>This is the weak link in the chain, which you are not supposed to recognize. Who compiles the various notes into the final agenda for discussion?</strong> </p>\n<p><strong>Ahhhh! Well, it is those who are running the meeting\u2026!!</strong></p>\n<p>How do you know that the ideas on your notes were included in the final result? You Don\u2019t! </p>\n<p>You may realize that your idea was not included and come to the conclusion that you were probably in the minority. Recognize that every other citizen member of this meeting has written his or her likes or dislikes on a similar sheet of paper and they, too, have no idea whether their ideas were \u201ccompiled\u201d into the final result! You don\u2019t even know if anyone\u2019s ideas are part of the final \u201cconclusions\u201d presented to the reassembled group as the \u201cconsensus\u201d of public opinion.</p>\n<p>Rarely does anyone challenge the process, since each concludes that he or she was in the minority and different from all the others.</p>\n<p>So, now, those who organized the meeting in the first place are able to tell the participants and the rest of the community that the conclusions, reached at the meeting, are the result of public participation.</p>\n<p>Actually, the desired conclusions had been established, in the back room, long before the meeting ever took place. There are variations in the technique to fit special situations but, in general, the procedure outlined above takes place.</p>\n<p>The natural question to ask here is: If the outcome was preordained before the meeting took place, why have the meeting? </p>\n<p><strong>Herein lies the genius of this Delphi Technique.<br/>\nIt is imperative that the general public believe that this program is theirs! They thought it up! They took part in its development! Their input was recognized!<br/>\nIf people believe that the program is theirs, they will support it.</strong></p>\n<p>If they get the slightest hint that the program is being imposed upon them, they will resist.<br/>\nThis very effective technique is being used, over and over and over, to change our form of government from the representative republic, intended by the Founding Fathers, into a \u201cparticipatory democracy.&#8221;</p>\n<p>Now, citizens chosen at large are manipulated into accepting preset outcomes while they believe that the input they provided produced the outcomes which are now theirs! The reality is that the final outcome was already determined long before any public meetings took place, determined by individuals unknown to the public. Can you say \u201cConspiracy?\u201d</p>\n<p>These \u201cChange Agents\u201d or \u201cFacilitators\u201d can be beaten! They may be beaten using their own methods against them.</p>\n<p>See how at the link above.</p>\n\t\t\t\t</div><!-- .comment-content -->\n\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"reply\"><a rel='nofollow' class='comment-reply-link' href='https://www.darkmoon.me/2017/who-is-destroying-america/?replytocom=948135#respond' onclick='return addComment.moveForm( \"div-comment-948135\", \"948135\", \"respond\", \"61343\" )' aria-label='Reply to Pat'>Reply</a></div>\t\t\t</article><!-- .comment-body -->\n<ol class=\"children\">\n\t\t<li id=\"comment-948136\" class=\"comment odd alt depth-2 parent\">\n\t\t\t<article id=\"div-comment-948136\" class=\"comment-body\">\n\t\t\t\t<footer class=\"comment-meta\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"comment-author vcard\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<img alt='' src='https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/29e9539d5b9a7f4c5a00683fe97e6813?s=60&#038;d=mm&#038;r=pg' srcset='https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/29e9539d5b9a7f4c5a00683fe97e6813?s=120&amp;d=mm&amp;r=pg 2x' class='avatar avatar-60 photo' height='60' width='60'/>\t\t\t\t\t\t<b class=\"fn\">Flopot</b> <span class=\"says\">says:</span>\t\t\t\t\t</div><!-- .comment-author -->\n\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"comment-metadata\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<a href=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/2017/who-is-destroying-america/#comment-948136\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<time datetime=\"2017-02-28T17:23:43+00:00\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tFebruary 28, 2017 at 5:23 pm\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</time>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t</a>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div><!-- .comment-metadata -->\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</footer><!-- .comment-meta -->\n\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"comment-content\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<p>@Pat</p>\n<p>What manipulation?
